	borrow_money = {
		#Scope: Country
		#Borrows money. Automatically caps at the maximum amount you can borrow.
		#INPUT:
			#borrow_money_temp - Amount of money to borrow. Non-integer amounts are accepted but integers are preferable
			#country_temp - Which country to specifically borrow from, set to 0 to borrow money from any country
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { borrow_money_temp > 0 }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = borrow_money_temp }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = borrow_temp
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = country_temp
				}
				#Borrow from Locals
				set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = borrow_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 1000 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { borrow_temp_k > national_bank_amount_left_k }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = national_bank_amount_left_k }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { borrow_temp_k < 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = borrow_temp_k }
					multiply_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = 1000 }
					add_to_variable = { treasury = borrow_temp }
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country value = THIS }
						}
						for_each_loop = {
							array = debt_to_bank_country
							value = cc
							index = iii
							break = bank_break

							if = {
								limit = {
									tag = cc
								}
								add_to_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { bank_break = 1 }
							}
						}
						for_each_loop = {
							array = money_lent_country
							value = cc
							index = iii
							break = lent_break

							if = {
								limit = {
									tag = cc
								}
								add_to_variable = { money_lent_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_to_array = { debt_to_bank_country = THIS }
						add_to_array = { debt_to_bank_amount = borrow_temp }
						add_to_array = { money_lent_country = THIS }
						add_to_array = { money_lent_amount = borrow_temp }
					}

				}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { country_temp = 0  }
				}
				set_variable = { borrow_money_amount_left = borrow_temp }
				#Borrow from Cheapest Banks
				for_each_loop = {
					array = global_bank_countries
					index = ii
					value = country_bank_temp
					break = bb

					set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = borrow_money_amount_left }
					divide_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 1000 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							tag = country_bank_temp
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { borrow_temp_k > national_bank_amount_left_k }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = national_bank_amount_left_k }
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { national_bank_amount_left_k_temp = national_bank_amount_left_k }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { national_bank_amount_left_k_temp = 1 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { borrow_temp_k > national_bank_amount_left_k_temp }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = national_bank_amount_left_k_temp }
						}
					}

					#Next Cheapest
					set_temp_variable = { ii_temp = ii }
					add_to_temp_variable = { ii_temp = 1 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { ii_temp < global_bank_countries^num }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { interest_rate_temp = global_bank_interest_rate^ii_temp }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { interest_rate_temp = global_bank_interest_rate^ii }
						add_to_temp_variable = { interest_rate_temp = global.loan_scarcity_increase_willingness }

						set_temp_variable = { borrow_limit_temp_k = country_bank_temp:national_bank_amount_k }
						divide_temp_variable = { borrow_limit_temp_k = global.loan_scarcity_rate }
						multiply_temp_variable = { borrow_limit_temp_k = interest_rate_temp }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { borrow_temp_k > borrow_limit_temp_k }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = borrow_limit_temp_k }
						}
					}
					
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { borrow_temp_k < 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = borrow_temp_k }
						multiply_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = 1000 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_in_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country value = country_bank_temp }
							}
							for_each_loop = {
								array = debt_to_bank_country
								value = cc
								index = iii
								break = bank_break

								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { cc = country_bank_temp }
									}
									add_to_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
									set_temp_variable = { bank_break = 1 }
								}
							}
							for_each_loop = {
								array = country_bank_temp:money_lent_country
								value = cc
								index = iii
								break = lent_break

								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { cc = country_bank_temp }
									}
									add_to_variable = { cc:money_lent_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
									set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							add_to_array = { debt_to_bank_country = country_bank_temp }
							add_to_array = { debt_to_bank_amount = borrow_temp }
							add_to_array = { country_bank_temp:money_lent_country = THIS }
							add_to_array = { country_bank_temp:money_lent_amount = borrow_temp }
						}
						add_to_variable = { treasury = borrow_temp }
						subtract_from_variable = { borrow_money_amount_left = borrow_temp }

						national_bank_update = yes
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { borrow_money_amount_left < 0.001 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { country_temp > 1000000 }
				}
				#Borrow from foreign country
				var:country_temp = {
					set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = borrow_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 1000 }
					set_temp_variable = { national_bank_amount_left_k_temp = national_bank_amount_left_k }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { national_bank_amount_left_k_temp = 1 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { borrow_temp_k > national_bank_amount_left_k_temp }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = national_bank_amount_left_k_temp }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { borrow_temp_k < 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp_k = 0 }
					}
					else = {

						set_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = borrow_temp_k }
						multiply_temp_variable = { borrow_temp = 1000 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_in_array = { array = PREV.debt_to_bank_country value = THIS }
							}
							for_each_loop = {
								array = PREV.debt_to_bank_country
								value = cc
								index = iii
								break = bank_break

								if = {
									limit = {
										tag = cc
									}
									add_to_variable = { PREV.debt_to_bank_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
									set_temp_variable = { bank_break = 1 }
								}
							}
							for_each_loop = {
								array = money_lent_country
								value = cc
								index = iii
								break = lent_break

								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { cc = PREV }
									}
									add_to_variable = { money_lent_amount^iii = borrow_temp }
									set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
								}
							}
						}
						else = {
							add_to_array = { PREV.debt_to_bank_country = THIS }
							add_to_array = { PREV.debt_to_bank_amount = borrow_temp }
							add_to_array = { money_lent_country = PREV }
							add_to_array = { money_lent_amount = borrow_temp }
						}
						add_to_variable = { PREV.treasury = borrow_temp }

						national_bank_update = yes
					}
				}
			}

			national_debt_update = yes
			national_bank_update = yes
		}
	}
	repay_debt = {
		#Scope: Country
		#Repays oustanding debt. Automatically caps at treasury amount.
		#INPUT:
			#debt_repayment_temp - Amount of debt to repay. Non-integer amounts are accepted but integers are preferable
			#country_temp - Which country to specifically repay to, set to 0 to repay debts owed to any country
			#			  - If the repay amount is higher than the owed amount, only the owed amount is payed. The excess is not payed out further
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 1 }
				check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp > 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp > treasury }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = treasury }
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = 0.5 }
			round_temp_variable = debt_repayment_temp

			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = country_temp
				}
				
				#Paying back to locals
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp > debt_to_national_bank }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_to_national_bank }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = debt_repayment_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 1000 }
				add_to_variable = { national_bank_amount_left_k = debt_repayment_temp_k }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k < 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country value = THIS }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_repayment_temp_k }
						multiply_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = 1000 }
						subtract_from_variable = { treasury = debt_repayment_temp }

						for_each_loop = {
							array = debt_to_bank_country
							value = cc
							index = iii
							break = bank_break

							if = {
								limit = {
									tag = cc
								}
								subtract_from_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^iii = debt_repayment_temp }
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^iii < 0.001 }
									}
									remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_amount index = iii }
									remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country index = iii }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { bank_break = 1 }
							}
						}
						for_each_loop = {
							array = money_lent_country
							value = cc
							index = iii
							break = lent_break

							if = {
								limit = {
									tag = cc
								}
								subtract_from_variable = { money_lent_amount^iii = debt_repayment_temp }
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { money_lent_amount^iii < 0.001 }
									}
									remove_from_array = { array = money_lent_amount index = iii }
									remove_from_array = { array = money_lent_country index = iii }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
							}
						}
						national_debt_update = yes
						national_bank_update = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { country_temp = 0  }
				}
				set_variable = { debt_repayment_amount_left = debt_repayment_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { length_temp = debt_to_bank_country^ii }
				set_temp_variable = { ii = 0 }
				#Repay to Banks with highest interest rates
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { ii < length_temp }
					}
					break = bb
					set_temp_variable = { length_temp = debt_to_bank_country^num }
					set_temp_variable = { country_bank_temp = debt_to_bank_country^ii }
					
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_repayment_amount_left }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp > debt_to_bank_amount^ii }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_to_bank_amount^ii }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = debt_repayment_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 1000 }

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k < 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_repayment_temp_k }
						multiply_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = 1000 }
						
						subtract_from_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^ii = debt_repayment_temp }
						set_variable = { var1 = debt_to_bank_amount^ii }
						for_each_loop = {
							array = country_bank_temp:money_lent_country
							value = cc
							index = iii
							break = lent_break

							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { cc = THIS }
								}
								subtract_from_variable = { country_bank_temp:money_lent_amount^iii = debt_repayment_temp }
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { country_bank_temp:money_lent_amount^iii < 0.001 }
									}
									remove_from_array = { array = country_bank_temp:money_lent_amount index = iii }
									remove_from_array = { array = country_bank_temp:money_lent_country index = iii }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
							}
						}
						subtract_from_variable = { treasury = debt_repayment_temp }
						subtract_from_variable = { debt_repayment_amount_left = debt_repayment_temp }
						var:country_bank_temp = {
							national_bank_update = yes
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^ii < 0.001 }
							}
							remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_amount index = ii }
							remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country index = ii }
						}
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { ii = 1 }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { debt_repayment_amount_left < 0.001 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
						}
					}
					add_to_temp_variable = { ii = 1 }
				}
				national_debt_update = yes
				national_bank_update = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { country_temp > 1000000 }
				}
				#Repay to a foreign country's bank				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp > debt_to_bank_amount^ii }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_to_bank_amount^ii }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = debt_repayment_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 1000 }

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k < 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp_k = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = debt_repayment_temp_k }
					multiply_temp_variable = { debt_repayment_temp = 1000 }
					
					subtract_from_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^ii = debt_repayment_temp }
					for_each_loop = {
						array = country_temp:money_lent_country
						value = cc
						index = iii
						break = lent_break

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { cc = THIS }
							}
							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:money_lent_amount^iii = debt_repayment_temp }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { country_temp:money_lent_amount^iii < 0.001 }
								}
								remove_from_array = { array = country_temp:money_lent_amount index = iii }
								remove_from_array = { array = country_temp:money_lent_country index = iii }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { lent_break = 1 }
						}
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { treasury = debt_repayment_temp }
					var:country_temp = {
						national_bank_update = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { debt_to_bank_amount^ii < 0.001 }
						}
						remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_amount index = ii }
						remove_from_array = { array = debt_to_bank_country index = ii }
					}

					national_debt_update = yes
					national_bank_update = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	new_trade_route = {
		#Scope: Country
		#Sets up an import route from country_temp to this country.
		#INPUT:
			#amount_temp
			#country_temp
			#resource_temp
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { amount_temp > 0 }
				check_variable = { resource_temp > -1 }
				check_variable = { resource_temp < 7 }
			}

			if = { #Any Country
				limit = {
					check_variable = { country_temp = 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { imp_quota = amount_temp }

				if = { #life_goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 0 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.life_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk
				
						set_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_quota }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > life_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = life_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { imp_quota > imp_amount_temp } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
									check_variable = { global.life_goods_price < country_temp:life_goods_price } #Breaks if country exceeds life goods limit
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
							}

							add_to_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
							set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							calculate_international_trade = yes

							add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #everyday_goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 1 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk
				
						set_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_quota }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:everyday_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:everyday_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > everyday_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = everyday_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { imp_quota > imp_amount_temp } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
									check_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price < country_temp:everyday_goods_price } #Breaks if country exceeds everyday goods limit
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
							}

							add_to_array = { everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
							set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							calculate_international_trade = yes

							add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:everyday_goods_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #luxury_goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 2 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk
				
						set_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_quota }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:luxury_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:luxury_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > luxury_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = luxury_goods_trade_step_amount }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { imp_quota > imp_amount_temp } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
									check_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price < country_temp:luxury_goods_price } #Breaks if country exceeds luxury goods limit
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
							}

							add_to_array = { luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
							set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							calculate_international_trade = yes

							add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value = luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:luxury_goods_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #services
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 3 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.services_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk
				
						set_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_quota }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:services_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:services_trade_step_amount }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > services_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = services_trade_step_amount }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { imp_quota > imp_amount_temp } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
									check_variable = { global.services_price < country_temp:services_price } #Breaks if country exceeds services goods limit
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { services_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
							}

							add_to_array = { services_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
							set_variable = { services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { services_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							calculate_international_trade = yes

							add_to_variable = { services_global_trade_amount = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { services_global_trade_value = services_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:services_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { services_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_amount = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { services_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { services_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { services_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #raw_goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 4 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk
				
						set_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_quota }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:raw_goods_trade_step_amount }

							limit = {
								check_variable = { this_temp > raw_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = raw_goods_trade_step_amount }

						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { imp_quota > imp_amount_temp } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
									check_variable = { global.raw_goods_price < country_temp:raw_goods_price } #Breaks if country exceeds raw goods limit
								}
							}
							set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_in_array = { raw_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
							}

							add_to_array = { raw_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
							set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							calculate_international_trade = yes

							add_to_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_amount = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_value = raw_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:raw_goods_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_amount = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #industrial_goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 5 }
					}

					#Loops thru cheapest countries to buy from
					for_each_loop = {
						array = global.industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = ch_brk

							set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
							set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

							add_to_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_amount = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }

							set_temp_variable = { gt_av = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:industrial_goods_price }
							subtract_from_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_amount = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

							add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = this_temp }
						}
						else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
							#Skip if trade is locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_variable = { button_trade_amount = this_temp }
								set_temp_variable = { trade_route_country = country_temp }
								verify_button_trade_amount = yes
								change_trade = yes

								add_to_temp_variable = { imp_amount_temp = button_trade_amount }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #Specific Country
				if = { #Life Goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 0 }
					}
					
					add_to_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
					set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
					set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

					calculate_international_trade = yes

					add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
				else_if = { #Everyday Goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 1 }
					}
					
					add_to_array = { everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
					set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
					set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

					calculate_international_trade = yes

					add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:everyday_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
				else_if = { #Luxury Goods
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 2 }
					}
					
					add_to_array = { luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
					set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
					set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

					calculate_international_trade = yes

					add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value = luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:luxury_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }

				}
				else_if = { #Services
					limit = {
						check_variable = { resource_temp = 3 }
					}
					
					add_to_array = { services_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
					set_variable = { services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
					set_variable = { services_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }

					add_to_variable = { services_global_trade_amount = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }

					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:services_price }

					add_to_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
				var:country_temp = {
					calculate_national_supply_demand = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				update_global_trade_display = yes
				update_new_trade_route = yes
			}
			calculate_national_supply_demand = yes
		}
	}
	change_trade = {
		#Input: button_trade_amount, country_temp, resource_temp

		if = { #Life Goods
			limit = {
				check_variable = { resource_temp = 0 }
			}
			
			subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = button_trade_amount }
				
			calculate_international_trade = yes
			
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
			subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
		}
		else_if = { #Everyday Goods
			limit = {
				check_variable = { resource_temp = 1 }
			}
			
			subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { gt_av = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:everyday_goods_price }
			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = button_trade_amount }

			subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }

			multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:everyday_goods_price }
			subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

	delete_trade = {
		#Input: country_temp, resource_temp

		if = { #Life Goods
			limit = {
				check_variable = { resource_temp = 0 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
			set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			remove_from_array = {
				array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = country_temp
			}
			clear_variable = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp
			clear_variable = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp
			clear_variable = life_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp
			clear_variable = life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp

			var:country_temp = {
				calculate_national_supply_demand = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Everyday Goods
			limit = {
				check_variable = { resource_temp = 1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }

			add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
			subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

			remove_from_array = {
				array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = i
			}
			clear_variable = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp
			clear_variable = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp

			}
