#Supply, Demand, Price
	calculate_global_price = {
		#Global Scope
		set_variable = { global.life_goods_price = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.services_price = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.raw_goods_price = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price = 0 }
		
		set_variable = { global.life_goods_supply = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.everyday_goods_supply = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.luxury_goods_supply = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.services_supply = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.raw_goods_supply = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.industrial_goods_supply = 0 }

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.econ_order_array
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = life_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = life_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.life_goods_price = p_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = everyday_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = everyday_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price = p_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = luxury_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = luxury_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price = p_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = services_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = services_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.services_price = p_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = raw_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = raw_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.raw_goods_price = p_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { p_temp = industrial_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { p_temp = industrial_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { p_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price = p_temp }

			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = life_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.life_goods_supply = s_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = everyday_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.everyday_goods_supply = s_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = luxury_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.luxury_goods_supply = s_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = services_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.services_supply = s_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = raw_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.raw_goods_supply = s_temp }
			
			set_temp_variable = { s_temp = industrial_goods_supply }
			divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1000 }
			add_to_variable = { global.industrial_goods_supply = s_temp }
		}

		divide_variable = { global.life_goods_price = global.life_goods_supply }
		divide_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price = global.everyday_goods_supply }
		divide_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price = global.luxury_goods_supply }
		divide_variable = { global.services_price = global.services_supply }
		divide_variable = { global.raw_goods_price = global.raw_goods_supply }
		divide_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price = global.industrial_goods_supply }

		set_variable = { global.life_goods_price_l = global.life_goods_price }
		divide_variable = { global.life_goods_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.life_goods_price_u = global.life_goods_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.life_goods_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
		
		set_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price_l = global.everyday_goods_price }
		divide_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price_u = global.everyday_goods_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.everyday_goods_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
		
		set_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price_l = global.luxury_goods_price }
		divide_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price_u = global.luxury_goods_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.luxury_goods_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
		
		set_variable = { global.services_price_l = global.services_price }
		divide_variable = { global.services_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.services_price_u = global.services_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.services_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
		
		set_variable = { global.raw_goods_price_l = global.raw_goods_price }
		divide_variable = { global.raw_goods_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.raw_goods_price_u = global.raw_goods_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.raw_goods_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
		
		set_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price_l = global.industrial_goods_price }
		divide_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price_l = global.price_bound_factor }
		set_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price_u = global.industrial_goods_price }
		multiply_variable = { global.industrial_goods_price_u = global.price_bound_factor }
	}
	calculate_supply_demand_at_global_price = {

		every_controlled_state = {
			set_variable = { life_goods_price = global.life_goods_price }
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = global.everyday_goods_price }
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = global.luxury_goods_price }
			set_variable = { services_price = global.services_price }
			set_variable = { raw_goods_price = global.raw_goods_price }
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = global.industrial_goods_price }
			
			calculate_demand = yes #Do first
			update_production_maintenance = yes #Do just after Demand
			calculate_supply = yes #Do just after Production
		}
		calculate_national_supply_demand = yes

		set_variable = { life_goods_supply_gp = life_goods_supply }
		set_variable = { everyday_goods_supply_gp = everyday_goods_supply }
		set_variable = { luxury_goods_supply_gp = luxury_goods_supply }
		set_variable = { services_supply_gp = services_supply }
		set_variable = { raw_goods_supply_gp = raw_goods_supply }
		set_variable = { industrial_goods_supply_gp = industrial_goods_supply }
		
		set_variable = { life_goods_demand_gp = life_goods_demand }
		set_variable = { everyday_goods_demand_gp = everyday_goods_demand }
		set_variable = { luxury_goods_demand_gp = luxury_goods_demand }
		set_variable = { services_demand_gp = services_demand }
		set_variable = { raw_goods_demand_gp = raw_goods_demand }
		set_variable = { industrial_goods_demand_gp = industrial_goods_demand }

		every_controlled_state = {

			set_variable = { life_goods_price = PREV.life_goods_price }
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = PREV.everyday_goods_price }
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = PREV.luxury_goods_price }
			set_variable = { services_price = PREV.services_price }
			set_variable = { raw_goods_price = PREV.raw_goods_price }
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = PREV.industrial_goods_price }
			
			calculate_demand = yes #Do first
			update_production_maintenance = yes #Do just after Demand
			calculate_supply = yes #Do just after Production
		}
		calculate_national_supply_demand = yes
	}
	calculate_global_trade_supply = {
		#Any (Global) Scope
		#Counts up all the supply exchange from trade

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.econ_order_array

			calculate_international_trade = yes
			
			set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = 0 } #Positive: Goods Bought / Negative: Goods Sold - Note, this only applies in this effect. It's always positive elsewhere.
			set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = 0 } #Positive: Amount Recieved / Negative: Amount Paid
			set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }

			set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = 0 }
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = 0 }
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }

			set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = 0 }
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value = 0 }
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }

			set_variable = { services_global_trade_amount = 0 }
			set_variable = { services_global_trade_value = 0 }
			set_variable = { services_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }

			set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_amount = 0 }
			set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_value = 0 }
			set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }

			set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_amount = 0 }
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_value = 0 }
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = 0 }
		}

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.econ_order_array

			#Life Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:life_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_amount = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
			#Everyday Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value = everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:everyday_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_amount = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:everyday_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
			#Luxury Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value = luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:luxury_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_amount = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:luxury_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
			#Raw Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_amount = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_value = raw_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:raw_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_amount = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:raw_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
			#Industrial Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_amount = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_value = industrial_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:industrial_goods_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_amount = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:industrial_goods_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
			#Services
				for_each_loop = {
					array = services_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					add_to_variable = { services_global_trade_amount = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					subtract_from_variable = { services_global_trade_value = services_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
					set_temp_variable = { gt_av = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gt_av = country_temp:services_price }
					subtract_from_variable = { services_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }

					subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_amount = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_value = gt_av }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:services_global_trade_actual_value = gt_av }
				}
			#
		}
	}

	calculate_trade_neighbors = {
		clear_array = global_trade_neighbor_array

		every_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { global.econ_order_array = THIS }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV.PREV.PREV
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { PREV.global_trade_neighbor_array = THIS }
			}
		}
	}

	calculate_trade_step_size = {
		#Country Scope

		#Life Goods
			set_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount = life_goods_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount = life_goods_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = life_goods_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 40 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { life_goods_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
		#Everyday Goods
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount = everyday_goods_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount = everyday_goods_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = everyday_goods_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
		#Luxury Goods
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount = luxury_goods_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount = luxury_goods_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = luxury_goods_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
		#Services
			set_variable = { services_trade_step_amount = services_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { services_trade_step_amount = services_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { services_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { services_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { services_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = services_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { services_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { services_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
		#Raw Goods
			set_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount = raw_goods_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount = raw_goods_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = raw_goods_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { raw_goods_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
		#Industrial Goods
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount = industrial_goods_demand }
			subtract_from_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount = industrial_goods_demand_gp }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount < 0 }
				}
				multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount = -1 }
			}
			divide_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount = 5 }

			set_temp_variable = { gtsa = industrial_goods_demand_gp }
			divide_temp_variable = { gtsa = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount < gtsa }
				}
				set_variable = { industrial_goods_trade_step_amount = gtsa }
			}
		#
	}

	ai_international_trade_calc = {
		#Country Scope
		#TODO - Manually add trade relations & update supply

		#Life Goods
			set_temp_variable = { resource_temp = 0 }

			set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
			add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
			set_temp_variable = { global_true_price = global.life_goods_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { global_true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
			divide_temp_variable = { global_true_price = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
			}

			set_temp_variable = { U_price_temp = global_true_price }
			multiply_temp_variable = { U_price_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { L_price_temp = global_true_price }
			divide_temp_variable = { L_price_temp = 1 }
			if = { #Import More
				limit = {
					check_variable = { U_price_temp < life_goods_price }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { import_quota = life_goods_demand_gp }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_quota = life_goods_demand }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { import_quota > life_goods_trade_step_amount }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { import_quota = life_goods_trade_step_amount }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						set_temp_variable = { s_temp = life_goods_supply }
						divide_temp_variable = { s_temp = 1.1 }
						check_variable = { s_temp > life_goods_demand_gp }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { import_quota = 0 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { imported_amount = 0 }

				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { import_quota > 0.01 }
					}

					#Priority trading partners get priority
					for_each_loop = {
						array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
						value = country_temp
						index = iii
						break = cheapest_brk

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 5 }
							}

							set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
							add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
							add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { lgp = country_temp:life_goods_price }
							multiply_temp_variable = { lgp = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
							divide_temp_variable = { lgp = 100 }

							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { imported_amount < import_quota }
									check_variable = { lgp < L_price_temp }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = import_quota }
								if ={
									limit = {
										check_variable = { amount_temp > country_temp:life_goods_supply }
									}
									set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = country_temp:life_goods_supply }
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { amount_temp < 0 }
									}
									set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = 0 }
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { amount_temp > country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
									}
									set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
								}

								add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
								add_to_variable = { life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
								subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
								add_to_temp_variable = { imported_amount = amount_temp }
							}
						}
					}

					#Seeing who has better price
					set_temp_variable = { lowest_price = global.life_goods_global_trade_price_array^0 }
					set_temp_variable = { lc_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^0 }
					set_temp_variable = { lowest_price_trade_partners = lc_temp:life_goods_price }
					
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = lc_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = lc_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
					add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
					}
					multiply_temp_variable = { lowest_price_trade_partners = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { lowest_price_trade_partners = 100 }

					multiply_temp_variable = { lowest_price = 1.5 } #Only create a new trade partner if significant difference in price 
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								check_variable = { lowest_price < lowest_price_trade_partners }
								check_variable = { L_price_temp < lowest_price_trade_partners }
								check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array^num = 0 }
							}
						}
						#New Trade Partner
						for_each_loop = {
							array = global.life_goods_global_trade_country_array
							value = country_temp
							index = iii
							break = ch_brk
					
							set_temp_variable = { this_temp = import_quota }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { this_temp = imp_amount_temp }
							if ={
								limit = {
									check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:life_goods_supply }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:life_goods_supply }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { this_temp < 0 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { this_temp = 0 }
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
							}

							if = {
								limit = {
									OR = {
										NOT = { check_variable = { import_quota > imported_amount } } #Breaks if you exceed your trading amount
										check_variable = { global.life_goods_price < country_temp:life_goods_price } #Breaks if country exceeds life goods limit
									}
								}
								set_temp_variable = { ch_brk = 1 }
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { is_in_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp } } #Skips over countries you're already trading with
								}

								add_to_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = country_temp }
								set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
								set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 1 }
								add_to_variable = { life_goods_supply = this_temp }

								subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = this_temp }

								add_to_temp_variable = { imported_amount = this_temp }
							}
							else = { #If you're already trading w/ country
								#Skip if trade is locked
								if = {
									limit = {
										NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
										NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
										NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
									}
									if ={
										limit = {
											check_variable = { this_temp > country_temp:life_goods_supply }
										}
										set_temp_variable = { this_temp = country_temp:life_goods_supply }
									}
									if = {
										limit = {
											check_variable = { this_temp < 0 }
										}
										set_temp_variable = { this_temp = 0 }
									}
									add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = this_temp }
									add_to_variable = { life_goods_supply = this_temp }
									subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = this_temp }
									add_to_temp_variable = { imported_amount = this_temp }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						#Old Trade Partner

						for_each_loop = {
							array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
							value = country_temp
							index = iii
							break = cheapest_brk

							#Skip if locked
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 4 } }
									NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
								add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
								subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
								add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
									}
									set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { lgp = country_temp:life_goods_price }
								multiply_temp_variable = { lgp = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
								divide_temp_variable = { lgp = 100 }

								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = { imported_amount < import_quota }
										check_variable = { lgp < L_price_temp }
									}
									set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = import_quota }
									if ={
										limit = {
											check_variable = { amount_temp > country_temp:life_goods_supply }
										}
										set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = country_temp:life_goods_supply }
									}
									if = {
										limit = {
											check_variable = { amount_temp < 0 }
										}
										set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = 0 }
									}
									if = {
										limit = {
											check_variable = { amount_temp > country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
										}
										set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = country_temp:life_goods_trade_step_amount }
									}
									add_to_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
									add_to_variable = { life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
									subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
									add_to_temp_variable = { imported_amount = amount_temp }
								}
								else = {
									set_temp_variable = { cheapest_brk = 1 }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Import Less (if importing at all)
				limit = {
					check_variable = { U_price_temp > life_goods_price }
					check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array^num > 0 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { import_cessation_quota = life_goods_trade_step_amount }
				
				set_temp_variable = { start_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^num }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = {	start_temp = 1 }

				#Priority goes first
				for_loop_effect = {
					start = start_temp
					end = 0
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					add = -1
					value = ii
					break = expensive_brk

					set_temp_variable = { country_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^ii }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 6 }
							check_variable = { import_cessation_quota > 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = import_cessation_quota }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { amount_temp > life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
						}
						subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
						subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
						add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = amount_temp }

						subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_cessation_quota = amount_temp }
					}
				}


				for_loop_effect = {
					start = start_temp
					end = 0
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					add = -1
					value = ii
					break = expensive_brk

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { import_cessation_quota > 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { country_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^ii }
						#Skip if locked
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 5 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 3 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = import_cessation_quota }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { amount_temp > life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							}
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = amount_temp }

							subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_cessation_quota = amount_temp }
						}
					}		
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { expensive_brk = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Import Less from countries with who are more expensive 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array^num > 0 }
				}
				
				set_temp_variable = { start_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^num }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = {	start_temp = 1 }
				for_loop_effect = {
					start = start_temp
					end = 0
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					add = -1
					value = ii
					break = expensive_brk

					set_temp_variable = { country_temp = life_goods_global_trade_country_array^ii }
					#Skip if locked
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 5 } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 3 } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_lock_type_@var:country_temp = 2 } }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = country_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
						add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { lgp = country_temp:life_goods_price }
						multiply_temp_variable = { lgp = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
						divide_temp_variable = { lgp = 100 }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_price > lgp }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = life_goods_trade_step_amount }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = { amount_temp > life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
								}
								set_temp_variable = { amount_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
							}
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp = amount_temp }
							subtract_from_variable = { life_goods_supply = amount_temp }
							add_to_variable = { country_temp:life_goods_supply = amount_temp }

							subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_cessation_amount = amount_temp }
						}
						else = {
							set_temp_variable = { expensive_brk = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		#
	}

	calculate_international_trade = {
		#Country Scope

		#Life Goods
			for_each_loop = {
				array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#life_goods_global_trade_country_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:life_goods_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { life_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#
		#Everyday Goods
			for_each_loop = {
				array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array - SET
				#everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_array - SET
				#everyday_goods_global_trade_value_array
				#everyday_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:everyday_goods_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#
		#Luxury Goods
			for_each_loop = {
				array = luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array - SET
				#luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_array - SET
				#luxury_goods_global_trade_value_array
				#luxury_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:luxury_goods_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#
		#Services
			for_each_loop = {
				array = services_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#services_global_trade_country_array - SET
				#services_global_trade_amount_array - SET
				#services_global_trade_value_array
				#services_global_trade_shipping_cost_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { services_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = services_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:services_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { services_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { services_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { services_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { services_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = services_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#
		#Raw Goods
			for_each_loop = {
				array = raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#raw_goods_global_trade_country_array - SET
				#raw_goods_global_trade_amount_array - SET
				#raw_goods_global_trade_value_array
				#raw_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:raw_goods_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { raw_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#
		#Industrial Goods
			for_each_loop = {
				array = industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
				value = c_temp
				index = iii
				break = cheapest_brk

				#industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array - SET
				#industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_array - SET
				#industrial_goods_global_trade_value_array
				#industrial_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_array

				#Value
				set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = c_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
				add_to_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp < 10 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { net_tariff_percentage_temp = 10 }
				}

				set_temp_variable = { true_price = c_temp:industrial_goods_price }
				multiply_temp_variable = { true_price = net_tariff_percentage_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { true_price = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_value_@var:c_temp = true_price }

				#Shipping Cost
				if = { 
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global_trade_neighbor_array = c_temp }
					}
					set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { exporter_capital = c_temp:capital }
					var:exporter_capital = {
						set_variable = { PREV.shipping_distance = distance_to@PREV.capital } #This needs to be a normal variable
					}
					divide_variable = { shipping_distance = global.base_shipping_cost_divisor }
					set_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = modifier@shipping_cost_modifier }
					add_to_temp_variable = { modifier_temp = 1 }
					multiply_variable = { shipping_distance = modifier_temp }
					add_to_variable = { shipping_distance = 1 }

					set_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = shipping_distance }
					multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:c_temp = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:c_temp }
				}
			}
		#

		clear_variable = shipping_distance
		
		calculate_shipping_capacity = yes
	}
	calculate_shipping_capacity = {
		set_variable = { shipping_capacity = 0 }
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				any_province_building_level = {
					building = naval_base
					level > 1
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { PREV.shipping_capacity = 10 }
		}

		set_variable = { shipping_capacity = 1000000 } #TODO - based off ports
		set_variable = { shipping_stress = 0 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = life_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = everyday_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = luxury_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = services_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = services_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = raw_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
			value = country_temp
			add_to_variable = { shipping_stress = industrial_goods_global_trade_shipping_cost_@var:country_temp }
		}

		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { shipping_stress > shipping_capacity }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { shipping_penalty_temp = shipping_stress }
			divide_temp_variable = { shipping_penalty_temp = shipping_capacity }

			set_variable = { shipping_penalty = 1 }
			divide_variable = { shipping_penalty = shipping_penalty_temp }
			subtract_from_variable = { shipping_penalty = 1 }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { shipping_penalty = 0 }
		}
	}
	conduct_international_trade = {

		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.econ_order_array
			
			#Life Goods
				for_each_loop = {
					array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
					value = country_temp
					index = iii
					break = cheapest_brk

					#life_goods_global_trade_country_array

					set_temp_variable = { cost_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { cost_temp = country_temp:life_goods_price }

					#Tariffs/Subsidies
					set_temp_variable = { export_cost_temp = 100 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { export_cost_temp = country_temp:export_tariff_percentage }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { export_cost_temp = country_temp:export_subsidy_percentage }
					multiply_temp_variable = { export_cost_temp = cost_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { export_cost_temp = 100 }
					set_temp_variable = { export_value_temp = export_cost_temp }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { export_value_temp = cost_temp }

					set_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = 100 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = import_tariff_percentage }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }
					multiply_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = cost_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = 100 }
					set_temp_variable = { import_value_temp = import_cost_temp }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_value_temp = cost_temp }

					add_to_temp_variable = { cost_temp = export_value_temp }
					add_to_temp_variable = { cost_temp = import_value_temp }
					add_to_variable = { country_temp:treasury = export_value_temp }
					add_to_variable = { treasury = import_value_temp }

						limit = {
							check_variable = { export_value_temp > 0 }
						}

					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = { country_temp:actual_trade_subsidy_spending = export_value_temp }
					}

						limit = {
							check_variable = { import_value_temp > 0 }
						}
						add_to_variable = { actual_tariff_revenue = import_value_temp }

					subtract_from_temp_variable = { import_cost_temp = import_subsidy_percentage }

	sort_international_trade_array = {
		#Life Goods
			clear_temp_array = life_goods_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = life_goods_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				set_temp_variable = { pr_temp = life_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { pr_temp = life_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = life_goods_gt_price_temp_array
					index = ii
					value = vv
					break = bb

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { vv > pr_temp }
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = life_goods_gt_price_temp_array 
							value = pr_temp
							index = ii
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = life_goods_gt_country_temp_array 
							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}
						set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { life_goods_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { life_goods_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = life_goods_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = life_goods_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { life_goods_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		#Everyday Goods
			clear_temp_array = everyday_goods_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = everyday_goods_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii

					index = ii

						}

							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}

					}
				}

						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { everyday_goods_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { everyday_goods_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = everyday_goods_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { everyday_goods_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		#Luxury Goods
			clear_temp_array = luxury_goods_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = luxury_goods_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				set_temp_variable = { pr_temp = luxury_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { pr_temp = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = luxury_goods_gt_price_temp_array
					index = ii
					value = vv
					break = bb

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { vv > pr_temp }
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = luxury_goods_gt_price_temp_array 
							value = pr_temp
							index = ii
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = luxury_goods_gt_country_temp_array 
							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}
						set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { luxury_goods_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { luxury_goods_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = luxury_goods_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { luxury_goods_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		#Raw Goods
			clear_temp_array = raw_goods_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = raw_goods_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				set_temp_variable = { pr_temp = raw_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { pr_temp = raw_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = raw_goods_gt_price_temp_array
					index = ii
					value = vv
					break = bb

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { vv > pr_temp }
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = raw_goods_gt_price_temp_array 
							value = pr_temp
							index = ii
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = raw_goods_gt_country_temp_array 
							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}
						set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { raw_goods_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { raw_goods_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = raw_goods_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = raw_goods_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { raw_goods_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		#Industrial Goods
			clear_temp_array = industrial_goods_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = industrial_goods_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				set_temp_variable = { pr_temp = industrial_goods_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { pr_temp = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = industrial_goods_gt_price_temp_array
					index = ii
					value = vv
					break = bb

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { vv > pr_temp }
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = industrial_goods_gt_price_temp_array 
							value = pr_temp
							index = ii
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = industrial_goods_gt_country_temp_array 
							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}
						set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { industrial_goods_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { industrial_goods_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = industrial_goods_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { industrial_goods_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		#Services
			clear_temp_array = services_gt_price_temp_array
			clear_temp_array = services_gt_country_temp_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = services_global_trade_country_array
				index = iii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				set_temp_variable = { pr_temp = services_global_trade_value_@var:country_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { pr_temp = services_global_trade_amount_@var:country_temp }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = services_gt_price_temp_array
					index = ii
					value = vv
					break = bb

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { vv > pr_temp }
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = services_gt_price_temp_array 
							value = pr_temp
							index = ii
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { 
							array = services_gt_country_temp_array 
							value = cy_temp
							index = ii
						}
						set_temp_variable = { bb = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { bb = 0 }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { services_gt_price_temp_array = pr_temp }
					add_to_temp_array = { services_gt_country_temp_array = cy_temp }
				}
			}
			clear_array = services_global_trade_country_array
			for_each_loop = {
				array = services_gt_country_temp_array
				index = ii
				value = cy_temp
				break = st_brk

				add_to_array = { services_global_trade_country_array = cy_temp }
			}
		#
		calculate_international_trade = yes
	}

	adjust_national_price = {
		set_temp_variable = { brk_v = 0 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_supply = life_goods_demand } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_supply = everyday_goods_demand } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_supply = luxury_goods_demand } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { services_supply = services_demand } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_supply = raw_goods_demand } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_supply = industrial_goods_demand } }
				}
				check_variable = { brk_v < 5 }
			}
			#Changing Prices
				#Life Goods
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = life_goods_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = life_goods_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > life_goods_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < life_goods_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { life_goods_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = life_goods_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = life_goods_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { life_goods_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { life_goods_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { life_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { life_goods_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { life_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { life_goods_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { life_goods_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_price < global.life_goods_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { life_goods_price = global.life_goods_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_price > global.life_goods_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { life_goods_price = global.life_goods_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { life_goods_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { life_goods_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
				#Everyday Goods
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = everyday_goods_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = everyday_goods_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > everyday_goods_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < everyday_goods_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { everyday_goods_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = everyday_goods_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = everyday_goods_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { everyday_goods_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_price < global.everyday_goods_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = global.everyday_goods_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_price > global.everyday_goods_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = global.everyday_goods_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { everyday_goods_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
				#Luxury Goods
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = luxury_goods_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = luxury_goods_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > luxury_goods_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < luxury_goods_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { luxury_goods_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = luxury_goods_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = luxury_goods_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { luxury_goods_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_price < global.luxury_goods_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = global.luxury_goods_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_price > global.luxury_goods_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = global.luxury_goods_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { luxury_goods_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
				#Services
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = services_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = services_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > services_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < services_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { services_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { services_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = services_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = services_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { services_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { services_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { services_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { services_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { services_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { services_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { services_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_price < global.services_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { services_price = global.services_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_price > global.services_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { services_price = global.services_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { services_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { services_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
				#Raw Goods
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = raw_goods_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = raw_goods_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > raw_goods_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < raw_goods_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { raw_goods_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = raw_goods_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = raw_goods_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { raw_goods_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { raw_goods_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { raw_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { raw_goods_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { raw_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { raw_goods_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { raw_goods_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_price < global.raw_goods_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { raw_goods_price = global.raw_goods_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_price > global.raw_goods_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { raw_goods_price = global.raw_goods_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { raw_goods_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { raw_goods_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
				#Industrial Goods
					if = {
						limit = {
							set_temp_variable = { supply_low = industrial_goods_supply }
							divide_temp_variable = { supply_low = 1.03 }
							set_temp_variable = { supply_high = industrial_goods_supply }
							multiply_temp_variable = { supply_high = 1.03 }

							OR = {
								check_variable = { supply_low > industrial_goods_demand }
								check_variable = { supply_high < industrial_goods_demand }
							}
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_demand = 0 } }
								NOT = { check_variable = { industrial_goods_supply = 0 } }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = industrial_goods_demand }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = industrial_goods_supply }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							divide_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { multiplier_temp = 1 }
							multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_price = multiplier_temp }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_demand < 0.01 }
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_need > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_demand = 0 }
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_need > 0 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_price = 0.9 }
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_supply = 0 }
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_demand > 0.01 }
							}
							multiply_variable = { industrial_goods_price = 1.2 }
							add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 10 }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_price < global.industrial_goods_price_l }
							}
							set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = global.industrial_goods_price_l }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_price > global.industrial_goods_price_u }
							}
							set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = global.industrial_goods_price_u }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { industrial_goods_price < 0.01 }
							}
							set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = 0.01 }
						}
					}
				#
			#

			every_controlled_state = {

				set_variable = { life_goods_price = PREV.life_goods_price }
				set_variable = { everyday_goods_price = PREV.everyday_goods_price }
				set_variable = { luxury_goods_price = PREV.luxury_goods_price }
				set_variable = { services_price = PREV.services_price }
				set_variable = { raw_goods_price = PREV.raw_goods_price }
				set_variable = { industrial_goods_price = PREV.industrial_goods_price }
				
				calculate_demand = yes #Do first
				update_production_maintenance = yes #Do just after Demand
				calculate_supply = yes #Do just after Production
			}
			calculate_national_supply_demand = yes
			
			add_to_temp_variable = { brk_v = 1 }
		}
	}
	calculate_national_supply_demand = {
		#Doesn't calculate on the state side. Only gets the supply/demand on the national side

		reset_supply = yes
		reset_demand = yes
		#Reset Offers & Requests
			set_variable = { life_goods_offers = 0 }
			set_variable = { life_goods_requests = 0 }

			set_variable = { everyday_goods_offers = 0 }
			set_variable = { everyday_goods_requests = 0 }

			set_variable = { luxury_goods_offers = 0 }
			set_variable = { luxury_goods_requests = 0 }

			set_variable = { raw_goods_offers = 0 }
			set_variable = { raw_goods_requests = 0 }

			set_variable = { industrial_goods_offers = 0 }
			set_variable = { industrial_goods_requests = 0 }
		#

		#Govt Demand
			calculate_govt_demand = yes

			add_to_variable = { life_goods_demand = life_goods_government_demand }
			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_demand = everyday_goods_government_demand }
			add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_demand = luxury_goods_government_demand }	
			add_to_variable = { services_demand = services_government_demand }
			add_to_variable = { raw_goods_demand = raw_goods_government_demand }
			add_to_variable = { industrial_goods_demand = industrial_goods_government_demand }
			
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_need = life_goods_government_need }
			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_need = everyday_goods_government_need }
			add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_need = luxury_goods_government_need }	
			add_to_variable = { services_need = services_government_need }
			add_to_variable = { raw_goods_need = raw_goods_government_need }
			add_to_variable = { industrial_goods_need = industrial_goods_government_need }
		#
		
		#Trade
			add_to_variable = { life_goods_supply = life_goods_global_trade_amount }
			add_to_variable = { everyday_goods_supply = everyday_goods_global_trade_amount }
			add_to_variable = { luxury_goods_supply = luxury_goods_global_trade_amount }
			add_to_variable = { services_supply = services_global_trade_amount }
			add_to_variable = { raw_goods_supply = raw_goods_global_trade_amount }
			add_to_variable = { industrial_goods_supply = industrial_goods_global_trade_amount }
		#

		every_controlled_state = {
			#How many goods can be exchanged total
			set_temp_variable = { infra_cap = 10000 } #TODO: Infrastructure

			#Total amount of goods that should be exchanged
			set_temp_variable = { infra_stress = 0 }

			#Preliminary - Finding how much needs to be traded
				#Life Goods
					set_temp_variable = { life_goods_trade_temp = life_goods_supply }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { life_goods_trade_temp = life_goods_demand }
					set_variable = { lgs = life_goods_supply }
					set_variable = { lgd = life_goods_demand }
					add_to_variable = { PREV.life_goods_need = life_goods_need }

					if = {
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { life_goods_trade_temp > 0 } #More Supply
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { infra_stress = life_goods_trade_temp }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { life_goods_trade_temp < 0 } #More Demand
						}
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { infra_stress = life_goods_trade_temp }
					}
				#
				#Everyday Goods
					set_temp_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_temp = everyday_goods_supply }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_temp = everyday_goods_demand }
					add_to_variable = { PREV.everyday_goods_need = everyday_goods_need }

					if = {
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_temp > 0 } #More Supply
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { infra_stress = everyday_goods_trade_temp }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							check_variable = { everyday_goods_trade_temp < 0 } #More Demand
						}
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { infra_stress = everyday_goods_trade_temp }
					}
				#
				#Luxury Goods
					set_temp_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_temp = luxury_goods_supply }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { luxury_goods_trade_temp = luxury_goods_demand }
